You can also pay an additional 38 yuan to participate in the hand-painting activity, and you will get a unique hand-painted plate or cup. The staff are very enthusiastic and give away fruits. msg:There are not many high-end hotels in Dehua. This one is my first choice. It is a hotel under the Lusheng Group. Next to it is their ceramic factory. When staying in the hotel, you can apply for a free visit to their brand exhibition hall and a close-up view of their production workshop, which is very interesting. The hotel has a good sense of design, and the attitude of the front desk staff is very good. When checking in, I was informed that there was a construction site next door and there would be noise. They could help upgrade the room type to the relatively quiet other side for free. There are welcome fruits when checking in, beer and drinks in the refrigerator, coffee in the drawer, and tea bags and tea sets on the table. There is no extra charge for all, which is very generous. The breakfast is rich in variety and tastes good. The overall stay experience is very good. If I have the opportunity to come to Dehua again, I will definitely stay in this hotel! When checking out, the front desk lady also gave me a Lusheng brand mug as a souvenir. I can only say that this is also very spicy! ğŸ˜
